(herald "Session Binding Protocol (SBP)")

(comment "CPSA 3.6.6")
(comment "All input read from sbp.lsp")

(defprotocol sbp basic
  (defrole client
    (vars (cc id s cred answer data) (enc_cookie mesg) (c p name))
    (trace (send cc) (recv (cat id (pubk p))) (send (enc s (pubk p)))
      (send (enc id (hash s cc id))) (recv (enc cc (hash s cc id)))
      (send (enc (enc "login:" cred (privk c)) (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc "login-successful" enc_cookie (hash s cc id)))
      (send (enc "request" enc_cookie (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc (enc "answer:" answer (privk p)) (hash s cc id))))
    (uniq-gen cc s))
  (defrole proxy
    (vars (cc id s cred iv cookie answer sskey data) (c p name))
    (trace (recv cc) (send (cat id (pubk p))) (recv (enc s (pubk p)))
      (recv (enc id (hash s cc id))) (send (enc cc (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc (enc "login:" cred (privk c)) (hash s cc id)))
      (send
        (enc "login-successful" iv
          (enc cookie (hash sskey (hash s cc id))) (hash s cc id)))
      (recv
        (enc "request" iv (enc cookie (hash sskey (hash s cc id)))
          (hash s cc id)))
      (send (enc (enc "answer:" answer (privk p)) (hash s cc id))))
    (non-orig sskey)
    (uniq-gen id)))

(defskeleton sbp
  (vars (enc_cookie mesg) (cred answer cc id s data) (c p name))
  (defstrand client 9 (enc_cookie enc_cookie) (cc cc) (id id) (s s)
    (cred cred) (answer answer) (c c) (p p))
  (non-orig (privk c) (privk p))
  (uniq-gen cc s)
  (traces
    ((send cc) (recv (cat id (pubk p))) (send (enc s (pubk p)))
      (send (enc id (hash s cc id))) (recv (enc cc (hash s cc id)))
      (send (enc (enc "login:" cred (privk c)) (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc "login-successful" enc_cookie (hash s cc id)))
      (send (enc "request" enc_cookie (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc (enc "answer:" answer (privk p)) (hash s cc id)))))
  (label 0)
  (unrealized (0 4) (0 6) (0 8))
  (origs)
  (comment "3 in cohort - 3 not yet seen"))

(defskeleton sbp
  (vars (enc_cookie mesg) (cred answer id s data) (c p name))
  (defstrand client 9 (enc_cookie enc_cookie) (cc id) (id id) (s s)
    (cred cred) (answer answer) (c c) (p p))
  (non-orig (privk c) (privk p))
  (uniq-gen id s)
  (operation encryption-test (displaced 1 0 client 4)
    (enc id (hash s id id)) (0 4))
  (traces
    ((send id) (recv (cat id (pubk p))) (send (enc s (pubk p)))
      (send (enc id (hash s id id))) (recv (enc id (hash s id id)))
      (send (enc (enc "login:" cred (privk c)) (hash s id id)))
      (recv (enc "login-successful" enc_cookie (hash s id id)))
      (send (enc "request" enc_cookie (hash s id id)))
      (recv (enc (enc "answer:" answer (privk p)) (hash s id id)))))
  (label 1)
  (parent 0)
  (unrealized (0 6) (0 8))
  (origs)
  (comment "1 in cohort - 1 not yet seen"))

(defskeleton sbp
  (vars (enc_cookie mesg) (cred answer cc id s data) (c p p-0 name))
  (defstrand client 9 (enc_cookie enc_cookie) (cc cc) (id id) (s s)
    (cred cred) (answer answer) (c c) (p p))
  (defstrand proxy 5 (cc cc) (id id) (s s) (p p-0))
  (precedes ((0 0) (1 0)) ((0 2) (1 2)) ((1 1) (0 1)) ((1 4) (0 4)))
  (non-orig (privk c) (privk p))
  (uniq-gen cc id s)
  (operation encryption-test (added-strand proxy 5)
    (enc cc (hash s cc id)) (0 4))
  (traces
    ((send cc) (recv (cat id (pubk p))) (send (enc s (pubk p)))
      (send (enc id (hash s cc id))) (recv (enc cc (hash s cc id)))
      (send (enc (enc "login:" cred (privk c)) (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc "login-successful" enc_cookie (hash s cc id)))
      (send (enc "request" enc_cookie (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc (enc "answer:" answer (privk p)) (hash s cc id))))
    ((recv cc) (send (cat id (pubk p-0))) (recv (enc s (pubk p-0)))
      (recv (enc id (hash s cc id))) (send (enc cc (hash s cc id)))))
  (label 2)
  (parent 0)
  (unrealized (0 6) (0 8) (1 2) (1 3))
  (comment "1 in cohort - 1 not yet seen"))

(defskeleton sbp
  (vars (cred answer cc id s cred-0 iv cookie sskey data)
    (c c-0 p name))
  (defstrand client 9
    (enc_cookie (cat iv (enc cookie (hash sskey (hash s cc id)))))
    (cc cc) (id id) (s s) (cred cred) (answer answer) (c c) (p p))
  (defstrand proxy 7 (cc cc) (id id) (s s) (cred cred-0) (iv iv)
    (cookie cookie) (sskey sskey) (c c-0) (p p))
  (precedes ((0 0) (1 0)) ((0 2) (1 2)) ((0 3) (1 3)) ((1 1) (0 1))
    ((1 4) (0 4)) ((1 6) (0 6)))
  (non-orig sskey (privk c) (privk p))
  (uniq-gen cc id s)
  (operation encryption-test (displaced 1 2 proxy 7)
    (enc "login-successful" iv (enc cookie (hash sskey (hash s cc id)))
      (hash s cc id)) (0 6))
  (traces
    ((send cc) (recv (cat id (pubk p))) (send (enc s (pubk p)))
      (send (enc id (hash s cc id))) (recv (enc cc (hash s cc id)))
      (send (enc (enc "login:" cred (privk c)) (hash s cc id)))
      (recv
        (enc "login-successful" iv
          (enc cookie (hash sskey (hash s cc id))) (hash s cc id)))
      (send
        (enc "request" iv (enc cookie (hash sskey (hash s cc id)))
          (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc (enc "answer:" answer (privk p)) (hash s cc id))))
    ((recv cc) (send (cat id (pubk p))) (recv (enc s (pubk p)))
      (recv (enc id (hash s cc id))) (send (enc cc (hash s cc id)))
      (recv (enc (enc "login:" cred-0 (privk c-0)) (hash s cc id)))
      (send
        (enc "login-successful" iv
          (enc cookie (hash sskey (hash s cc id))) (hash s cc id)))))
  (label 11)
  (parent 8)
  (unrealized (0 8) (1 5))
  (comment "2 in cohort - 2 not yet seen"))
